2025-09-16 18:51:20.534 +02:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (32ms) [Parameters=[@__date_Month_0='?' (DbType = Int32), @__date_Day_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__date_Date_2='?' (DbType = DateTime2)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [PublicHolidays] AS [p]
        WHERE ([p].[IsRecurring] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND DATEPART(month, [p].[Date]) = @__date_Month_0 AND DATEPART(day, [p].[Date]) = @__date_Day_1) OR ([p].[IsRecurring] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND CONVERT(date, [p].[Date]) = @__date_Date_2)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
